ARIE vol.044, 1921-1922


A.--List of copper plates examined during the year 1921-22.
1
Placement
M.R.Ry. Pendyala Venkata-subrahmanya Sastri, NationalCollege, Bandar, through theTahsildar of Bandar, Kistnadistrict.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 940 (inwords), Jyē-shṭa, Kṛish-ṇa-paksha,navamī, Sun-day.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Records the grant of the village [Tā]ḍipāḍi asan agrahāra and two tanks by the Malayachiefs Kāma-rāju Eṟama-rāju, ImmaḍiBeḍaṅga-rāju, Śōḍapa-rāju, Kaliyuga Kaṇ-ṇa-rāju and Mārvala Garuḍa to Naḍupa-Nāyaka the general of Chōḍaya-rāja. Therecord is written very indifferently.
2
Placement
M.R.Ry. Pendyala Venkata-subrahmanya Sastri, NationalCollege, Bandar, through thePresident, District Board,Godavari district.
Year
EasternChāḷukya
King
Indravarma-Mahārāja aliasTyāgadhēnu.
Date
…
Language and Script
Sanskrit in archaic Telugu characters
Remarks
Gift of the village Koṇḍanāgūru by the kingas a brahmadēya to the brahman Cheṇḍi-śarman of the Bhāradvāja-gōtra and theVājasanēya-charaṇa. The king is called thegrandson of Kīrtivarma-Mahārāja, and theson of Vishṇuvardhana-Mahārāja, i.e.,Kubja-Vishṇuvardhana.
3
Placement
The Revenue Divisional Officer,Ellore, Kistna district.
Year
Do.
King
Sarvalōkāśraya Śrī Vishṇu-vardhana-Mahārāja aliasRājarājadēva.
Date
2nd year
Language and Script
Sanskrit in Telugu characters
Remarks
Registers the gift of the governorship (manni-ya-nibaddham-ādhipatyam) over 1,000villages in Vēṅgīpura-vishaya to the chiefMummaḍi Bhīma of the Solar race, whowas a much favoured subordinate of theking. The king is said to have beencrowned in Tulā-lagna on Wednesday, thetenth day of the dark fortnight of Karka-ṭaka (Kuḷīra).
4
Placement
The Tahsildar of Karkala,through the Collector ofSouth Kanara.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1465, Śō-bhakṛit, ??Chaitra, śu.,4, Friday.
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
Registers an agreement given to KeravasiPāṇḍyapparasa by Tirumalarasa Chauṭaru,by which both the parties pledged them-selves to permanent alliance to help eachother against enemies and not to entertaintraitors from the other's camp. The witnessto the transaction was Nāḍubaḷi Māramma-Heggaḍe.
5
Placement
Do.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Do.
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
Records a similar agreement given by Pāṇḍyap-parasa, son of Chandaladēvī to Tiru-malarasa Chauṭaru. This is evidently theundertaking reciprocal to the above. The(Jaina) spiritual teacher Lalitakīrti-Bhaṭārais mentioned.
6

Do.
Year
…
King
…

Śaka 1450,Sarvadhāri,Vṛishabha,14, Monday.
Language and Script
Kanarese
Remarks
This is an agreement given to the Chavuṭachief of Tuḷuva and Nāḷina Tirumalarasaby Tirumalarasa Kinnika-Heggaḍe andNāḷina Kinnika-Nimittaru entering into analliance both offensive and defensive. Thetransaction was made in the presence ofŚrīmat Kṛishṇānanda-Oḍeya.

8

The Patel of Kap, throughthe Stationary DeputyTahsildar, Udipi, SouthKanara district.

King

Language and Script
Sanskrit & Kanarese
Remarks
Records the grant of some lands in the villageMai[lā]ra made by Tirumalarasa aliasMadda-Heggaḍe, the chief of Kāp and hissubordinate (?) Gaṇapaṇa-Sāmanta withthe co-operation of the people of Kāp,at the instance of Dēvachandradēva for thespiritual benefit of his guru Munichandra-dēva.
9
Placement
M.R.Ry. Uddi Nrisimha-charya of Kandukur, Mada-napalle taluk, Chittoordistrict, through the Kana-rese Assistant Mr. N.Laksh-minarayana Rao, M.A.
Year
Do.
King
Vīrapratāpa Veṅkaṭapatidēva-rāya.
Date
Śaka 1535, Pra-mādīcha,Vaiśākha,Śukla, dvā-daśī.
Language and Script
Sanskrit in Nandi-Nāgari
Remarks
Registers a gift of lands made by the kingto meet the expenses connected with certainfestivals of the god Veṅkaṭanātha on thePhaṇigiri hill, i.e., Śēshāchala (viz., Tiru-malai).
10
Placement
M.R.Ry. R.Hari Rao,Kumbhakonam, through theAssistant ArchaeologicalSuperintendent for Epi-graphy.
Year
TanjoreNāyaka.
King
Vijayarāghava
Date
Śaka 1578 (ex-pired) Man-matha, Mīna,Śukla, Paur-namāsyā,Friday.
Language and Script
Sanskrit in Telugu
Remarks
Registers the gift of a village called Alamēlu-maṅgāpuram as agrahāra to Vaishṇavabrahmans who were learned in the Vēdas.

Placement
On the south wall of the Nāgēśvaratemple at Serkad.
Year
Vijayanagara
King
[Ka]mpaṇa-Uḍaiyar
Date

Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the free colonization of the maḍaiviḷāgam bypeople, the taxes accruing there on being utilized for wor-ship in and repairs to the temple of Tirunāgīśvaram-uḍaya-Nāyaṉār at Śērkāḍu in Vaḷḷimalai-paṟṟu in Tuyil-nāḍu,a subdivision of Paḍuvūr-kōṭṭam, at the instance of themahāpradhāni Sōmappa-Uḍaiyar, for the continuity ofthe rule of Kampaṇa-Uḍaiyar. Aḍaippam Nāgappa hadthe record engraved on stone.

208
Placement
On the north wall of the centralshrine in the Bilvanāthēśvaratemple at Tiruvallam.
Year
Chōḷa
King
Rājakēsarivarman, [‘who destroyed theships at Kāndaḷūr-śālai’].
Date
13th year
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Registers that Araśūruḍaiyāṉ Īrāyiravaṉ Pallavayaṉ aliasMummuḍi-śōḻa Pōśaṉ, the supervisor of the temple ofTiruttīkkāli-Āḻvār at Tīkkāli-Vallam, in Mīyāṟu-nāḍu,a sub-division of Paḍuvūr-kōṭṭam, finding that one of thedirectors (gaṇattār) of the village had received 25 poṉ,weighed by the standard weight Dharmakaṭṭaḷai-tuḷai-niṟai, for burning a perpetual lamp founded by Śiṅga-pirāṭṭiyār and that his nephew or son-in-law (marumakaL)Śarvaḍichchaḍaṅgavi had neglected to maintain thelamp, now made a gift of 600 kuḻi of his land for continu-ing the charity.

1
Placement
On the north wall of the centralshrine in the Abhirāmēśvaratemple at Tiruvamattur, Villu-puram taluk, South Arcot district.
Year
Chōḷa

Date

Language and Script
